political_decisions = {
 ReleaseNZF= {
        picture = dreams_of_empire
        potential = {
                NOT = { exists = NZF}  has_country_flag = utilitymod_enable_release_nations any_owned_province = { is_core =NZF }
        }        
        allow = {
                ai = no                
        }
                effect = {                        
                        badboy = -2
                        any_owned = {
                                limit = { AND = {is_core = NZF NOT = {is_core = THIS}}} 
                                secede_province = NZF }
                        create_vassal = NZF
                        create_alliance = NZF
                        diplomatic_influence = { who = NZF value = 200 }
                        relation = { who = NZF value = 200 }
                }
        ai_will_do = { factor = 0 }
}

        potential = {
                NOT = { exists = KHO}  has_country_flag = utilitymod_enable_release_nations any_owned_province = { is_core =KHO }
        }        
        allow = {
                ai = no                
        }
                effect = {                        
                        badboy = -2
                        any_owned = {
                                limit = { AND = {is_core = KHO NOT = {is_core = THIS}}} 
                                secede_province = KHO }
                        create_vassal = KHO
                        create_alliance = KHO
                        diplomatic_influence = { who = KHO value = 200 }
                        relation = { who = KHO value = 200 }
                }
        ai_will_do = { factor = 0 }
}
